<p><em>Release date: December 3, 2025</em></p>
<p><strong>Highlights</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ“…Â Introducing <a href="/develop/api-reference/widgets/st.datetime_input"><code>st.datetime_input</code></a> to set date and time in a single widget.</li>
<li>ğŸ“©Â To avoid blocking your script, you can pass a callable to <a href="/develop/api-reference/widgets/st.download_button"><code>st.download_button</code></a> for on-demand download generation (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12942">#12942</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/5053">#5053</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¤Â <a href="/develop/api-reference/chat/st.chat_input"><code>st.chat_input</code></a> can optionally accept audio input (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12836">#12836</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/13054">#13054</a>).</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Notable Changes</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ¹Â You can configure keyboard shortcuts for <a href="/develop/api-reference/widgets/st.button">buttons</a> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12975">#12975</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/1291">#1291</a>).</li>
<li>â“Â You can now pass query parameters to <a href="/develop/api-reference/navigation/st.switch_page"><code>st.switch_page</code></a> and <a href="/develop/api-reference/widgets/st.page_link"><code>st.page_link</code></a> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/13027">#13027</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8102">#8102</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8112">#8112</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/13093">#13093</a>).</li>
<li>ã€°ï¸Â <a href='/develop/api-reference/text/st.html'><code>st.html</code></a> has a new <code>unsafe_allow_javascript</code> parameter to execute JavaScript (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12918">#12918</a>).</li>
<li>â¬†ï¸Â <a href="/develop/api-reference/data/st.metric"><code>st.metric</code></a> has a new <code>delta_arrow</code> parameter to configure the visibility and orientation of the delta arrow (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12982">#12982</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/4775">#4775</a>).</li>
<li>âŒ¨ï¸Â You can configure the horizontal alignment of <a href="/develop/api-reference/text/st.markdown"><code>st.markdown</code></a>, <code>st.caption</code>, <code>st.title</code>, <code>st.header</code>, <code>st.subheader</code>, and <code>st.text</code> with a new <code>text_alignment</code> parameter (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/13032">#13032</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/4109">#4109</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/13034">#13034</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/13036">#13036</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸŒ€Â You can use a spinner everywhere you can set an <code>icon</code> and in the <code>avatar</code> parameter of <a href="/develop/api-reference/chat/st.chat_message"><code>st.chat_message</code></a>. The spinner can&#x27;t be used as a page favicon (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/13045">#13045</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/6415">#6415</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ› ï¸Â You can now add tooltips to <a href="/develop/api-reference/text/st.badge"><code>st.badge</code></a> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12897">#12897</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/12878">#12878</a>). Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/marcolanfranchi">marcolanfranchi</a>!</li>
<li>ğŸ•³ï¸Â You can configure placeholder text for null values in <a href="/develop/api-reference/data/st.dataframe"><code>st.dataframe</code></a> and <a href="/develop/api-reference/data/st.data_editor"><code>st.data_editor</code></a> with a new <code>placeholder</code> parameter (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12968">#12968</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/7360">#7360</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ”‘Â To prevent widgets from resetting when you change a parameter, widgets are transitioning to an identity based only on their keys (if provided). The following widgets use only their key for their identity:<!-- -->
<ul>
<li><code>st.file_uploader</code></li>
<li><code>st.camera_input</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>â†•ï¸Â <code>st.plotly_chart</code> has a height parameter to use with flex containers (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12593">#12593</a>).</li>
<li>â†”ï¸Â <code>st.container</code>, <code>st.dataframe</code>, and <code>st.data_editor</code> support <code>width=&quot;content&quot;</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12848">#12848</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12875">#12875</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/12391">#12391</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸÂ Streamlit supports Python 3.14 and Vega-Altair 6!</li>
<li>ğŸ‘»Â <code>st.bokeh_chart</code> has been removed. Use the <code>streamlit-bokeh</code> custom component instead.</li>
<li>â˜ ï¸Â <code>**kwargs</code> is deprecated in <code>st.vega_lite_chart</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/13141">#13141</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ’©Â The <code>.add_rows()</code> method is under consideration for removal. Please leave feedback (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/13063">#13063</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ‘¥Â We&#x27;re improving community contributions by using a public workflow for discussing feature specs (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12248">#12248</a>).</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Other Changes</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸª¥Â For better performance, Streamlit uses <code>uvloop</code> if it&#x27;s installed (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/13047">#13047</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ§¼Â For improved performance, Markdown plugins are lazy loaded (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/13152">#13152</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ§½Â To improve load times, we reduced the bundle size (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/13071">#13071</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/13077">#13077</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/13099">#13099</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/13115">#13115</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/13128">#13128</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ›Â To improve performance, we&#x27;ve refactored session context data (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12788">#12788</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12789">#12789</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12790">#12790</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12791">#12791</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸš¿Â The hovering performance of <code>st.line_chart</code> was improved (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/13156">#13156</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/13154">#13154</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ§¹Â <code>st.metric</code> was optimized to prevent poor hovering performance with large data sets (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12983">#12983</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ‘½Â The <code>packaging</code> Python dependency is no longer version-capped (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/13073">#13073</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ«¥Â For clarity, Streamlit logs a warning if you try to hide a non-range index when using <code>st.data_editor</code> with <code>num_rows=&quot;dynamic&quot;</code>. A non-range index must be editable to add rows (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12978">#12978</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8263">#8263</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦‹Â Bug fix: Streamlit auth raises a warning instead of an error when browser back navigation revisits a consumed OAuth callback (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/13127">#13127</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/13101">#13101</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦€Â Bug fix: The WebSocket timeout was increased on Android to improve <code>st.file_uploader</code> performance (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/13132">#13132</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/11419">#11419</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦Â Bug fix: Query parameters are preserved when using browser back and forward navigation (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/13129">#13129</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/9279">#9279</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸŒÂ Bug fix: For custom components v2, the frontend key is correctly computed to be stable if it has a key in Python and otherwise change when its parameters change (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12950">#12950</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ•¸ï¸Â Bug fix: Empty code blocks in Markdown don&#x27;t display &quot;undefined&quot; (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/13074">#13074</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/12986">#12986</a>). <li>ğŸ¦—Â Bug fix: <code>st.feedback</code> is prevented from wrapping (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12970">#12970</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/12068">#12068</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦‚Â Bug fix: Custom components v2 don&#x27;t raise a warning when placeholders are replaced as a result of the initial manifest scan (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/13043">#13043</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/13042">#13042</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦ŸÂ Bug fix: <code>st.audio_input</code> has the correct padding for its waveform (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/13010">#13010</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦ Â Bug fix: The date and time icons in <code>st.data_editor</code> are visible in dark mode (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12994">#12994</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/12852">#12852</a>). <li>ğŸª°Â Bug fix: <code>st.pills</code> and <code>st.segmented_control</code> wrap correctly when <code>width=&quot;content&quot;</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12969">#12969</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/12067">#12067</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12879">#12879</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/12857">#12857</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸª³Â Bug fix: <code>st.color_picker</code> has a minimum width to prevent a pixel width below its intrinsic size (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12962">#12962</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/12872">#12872</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ•·ï¸Â Bug fix: Disabled widgets hide their borders (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12949">#12949</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸÂ <code>st.audio_input</code> and <code>st.chat_input</code> show a clearer message when microphone permissions are insufficient (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12914">#12914</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸÂ Bug fix: <code>st.navigation</code> uses the sidebar font and Streamlit falls back to its built-in fonts if a font can&#x27;t be found (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12948">#12948</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸœÂ Bug fix: <code>MultiselectColumn</code> doesn&#x27;t raise a <code>ValueError</code> when adding new rows in <code>st.data_editor</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12860">#12860</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12936">#12936</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/12815">#12815</a>). <li>ğŸ›Â Bug fix: <code>st.text_area</code> avoids negative height calculations that produce invalid CSS (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12891">#12891</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/12867">#12867</a>).</li>

<p><em>Release date: October 29, 2025</em></p>
<p><strong>Highlights</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ§©Â Announcing <a href="/develop/api-reference/custom-components/st.components.v2.component">custom components</a>, version 2! Easily create frameless custom UI with bidirectional data flow.</li>
<li>ğŸŒ—Â Introducing custom <a href="/develop/concepts/configuration/theming">light and dark theme</a> configuration! You can simultaneously define custom light and dark themes in your app.</li>
<li>ğŸ¨Â Announcing <a href="/develop/api-reference/configuration/config.toml#theme">reusable themes</a>! You can define a theme in a sharable file and use it as a base in other themes.</li>
<li>ğŸ’«Â Introducing <a href="/develop/api-reference/layout/st.space"><code>st.space</code></a> for adding vertical and horizontal spaces in your app.</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Notable Changes</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ”—Â New configuration options, <code>theme.codeTextColor</code> and <code>theme.linkColor</code>, let you configure the color of code and link text.</li>
<li>ğŸ“ŠÂ <a href="/develop/api-reference/data/st.column_config/st.column_config.progresscolumn"><code>ProgressColumn</code></a> has a new <code>color</code> parameter.</li>
<li>ğŸŒˆÂ You can set <code>color=&quot;auto&quot;</code> in <a href="/develop/api-reference/data/st.column_config/st.column_config.multiselectcolumn"><code>MultiselectColumn</code></a> to inherit colors from <code>theme.chartCategoricalColors</code>.</li>
<li>ğŸ“ŒÂ <code>MultiselectColumn</code> has a <code>pinned</code> parameter to match other column types.</li>
<li>â­Â You can set a <code>default</code> value for <a href="/develop/api-reference/widgets/st.feedback"><code>st.feedback</code></a> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12578">#12578</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/9469">#9469</a>). Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/andreasntr">andreasntr</a>!</li>
<li>ğŸ‘†Â <a href="/develop/api-reference/write-magic/st.write_stream"><code>st.write_stream</code></a> has a <code>cursor</code> parameter to set a custom cursor for the typewriter effect.</li>
<li>ğŸ¿Â <a href="/develop/api-reference/layout/st.popover"><code>st.popover</code></a> has a <code>type</code> parameter to match <code>st.button</code> styling options.</li>
<li>ğŸ”‘Â To prevent widgets from resetting when you change a parameter, widgets are transitioning to an identity based only on their keys (if provided). The following widgets use only their key for their identity:<!-- -->
<ul>
<li><code>st.color_picker</code></li>
<li><code>st.segmented_control</code></li>
<li><code>st.radio</code></li>
<li><code>st.audio_input</code></li>
<li><code>st.slider</code></li>
<li><code>st.select_slider</code></li>
<li><code>st.chat_input</code></li>
<li><code>st.feedback</code></li>
<li><code>st.pills</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>â†•ï¸Â <code>st.dataframe</code>, <code>st.data_editor</code>, <code>st.altair_chart</code>, <code>st.pydeck_chart</code>, and all simple charts have height parameters to use with flex containers.</li>
<li>â†”ï¸Â <code>st.plotly_chart</code>, <code>st.vega_lite_chart</code>, <code>st.altair_chart</code>, <code>st.pydeck_chart</code>, and all simple charts have width parameters to use with flex containers.</li>
<li>ğŸÂ Due to end of life, Python 3.9 is no longer supported.</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Other Changes</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>âš¡Â If you don&#x27;t pass a file to <code>streamlit run</code>, it will try <code>streamlit_app.py</code> by default (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12599">#12599</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¥·Â <code>st.dataframe</code> hides its index column by default when row selections are enabled (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12448">#12448</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/12237">#12237</a>). Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/plumol">plumol</a>!</li>
<li>ğŸ‘©â€ğŸ¨Â For compatibility with new theming options, the app settings menu no longer supports theme editing (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12648">#12648</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ‘‹Â The Streamlit hello app preloads its Python packages on its home page for a faster user experience (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12617">#12617</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ‘Â Slider thumbs don&#x27;t extend beyond the edge of their track (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12549">#12549</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/4284">#4284</a>).</li>
<li>â„¹ï¸Â Material icons and emojis were updated (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12669">#12669</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦ Â Bug fix: Pyplot charts render correctly in fragments, containers, and expanders (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12807">#12807</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/12678">#12678</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/12763">#12763</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸª°Â Bug fix: Dataframes correctly resize and align when using <code>width=&quot;content&quot;</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12682">#12682</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸª³Â Bug fix: Fuzzy search in select boxes is case insensitive (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12849">#12849</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/11724">#11724</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ•·ï¸Â Bug fix: 500 errors display correctly (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12845">#12845</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸÂ Bug fix: Deprecation warnings respect <code>client.showErrorDetails</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12794">#12794</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/12743">#12743</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸÂ Bug fix: Path handling in the file watcher was improved to prevent a <code>ValueError</code> in Windows environments (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12741">#12741</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/12731">#12731</a>).</li>

<li>ğŸ›Â Bug fix: Streamlit&#x27;s handling of Altair charts was improved for thread safety and prevention of an &quot;Unrecognized data set&quot; race condition (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12673">#12673</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11911">#11911</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/11342">#11342</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/11906">#11906</a>).</li>

<p><em>Release date: September 23, 2025</em></p>
<p><strong>Highlights</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ¤¹Â Introducing <a href="/develop/api-reference/data/st.column_config/st.column_config.multiselectcolumn"><code>MultiselectColumn</code></a> to configure colorful, editable lists in your dataframes.</li>
<li>ğŸ¨Â Announcing <a href="/develop/concepts/configuration/theming-customize-colors-and-borders#basic-color-palette">color palette</a> configuration options to set the exact shade of red, orange, yellow, green, blue, violet, and grey to use in Markdown, status elements, sparklines, <code>st.metric</code>, and <code>st.badge</code>.</li>
<li>ğŸ“ŠÂ <a href="/develop/api-reference/charts/st.bar_chart"><code>st.bar_chart</code></a> has a new <code>sort</code> parameter for conveniently sorting your bars.</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Notable Changes</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ”‘Â To prevent widgets from resetting when you change a parameter, widgets are transitioning to an identity based only on their keys (if provided). The following widgets use only their key for their identity:<!-- -->
<ul>
<li><code>st.button</code></li>
<li><code>st.download_button</code></li>
<li><code>st.form_submit_button</code></li>
<li><code>st.checkbox</code></li>
<li><code>st.toggle</code></li>
<li><code>st.text_area</code></li>
<li><code>st.text_input</code></li>
<li><code>st.number_input</code></li>
<li><code>st.time_input</code></li>
<li><code>st.date_input</code></li>
<li><code>st.selectbox</code></li>
<li><code>st.multiselect</code></li>
<li>Custom components</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>ğŸ–Œï¸Â You can configure the color of <a href="/develop/api-reference/data/st.column_config/st.column_config.areachartcolumn">chart columns</a>.</li>
<li>ğŸ”¢Â <a href="/develop/api-reference/data/st.metric"><code>st.metric</code></a> supports <code>decimal.Decimal</code> types (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12377">#12377</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/12308">#12308</a>). Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/aebrahim">aebrahim</a>!</li>
<li>ğŸ¤Â You can specify the sample rate for <a href="/develop/api-reference/widgets/st.audio_input"><code>st.audio_input</code></a>, and the default sample rate has been reduced to 16000 Hz.</li>
<li>âš™ï¸Â For clarity, in <a href="/develop/api-reference/charts/st.plotly_chart"><code>st.plotly_chart</code></a>, <code>**kwargs</code> is deprecated and replaced by <code>config</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12291">#12291</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/12280">#12280</a>). Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/zyfy29">zyfy29</a>!</li>
<li>ğŸ“ˆÂ <a href="/develop/api-reference/charts/st.line_chart"><code>st.line_chart</code></a> and <a href="/develop/api-reference/charts/st.graphviz_chart"><code>st.graphviz_chart</code></a> have <code>width</code> parameters to use with flex containers.</li>
<li>ğŸ”²Â You can configure <a href="/develop/api-reference/data/st.table"><code>st.table</code></a> borders to show all, only horizontal, or no lines.</li>
<li>ğŸ“‚Â You can specify a default tab in <a href="/develop/api-reference/layout/st.tabs"><code>st.tabs</code></a>.</li>
<li>ğŸŒÂ To use hosted fonts from providers like Google and Adobe, you can declare externally hosted fonts with a URL to their CSS file in <code>theme.font</code>, <code>theme.headingFont</code>, and <code>theme.codeFont</code>.</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Other Changes</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ§¹Â <code>**kwargs</code> has been removed from <code>st.write</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12375">#12375</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/12374">#12374</a>).</li>
<li>â±ï¸Â To prevent browser defaults from invalidating caches too soon, cache headers include the <code>max-age</code> and <code>immutable</code> directives (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12420">#12420</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ‘½Â Material icons were updated (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12473">#12473</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12535">#12535</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦‹Â Visual tweaks (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12348">#12348</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12367">#12367</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ‘»Â Bug fix: To correct a sequential navigation regression for <code>st.number_input</code>, some internal refactoring was reverted (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12547">#12547</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/12526">#12526</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦€Â Bug fix: Custom components respect zero-size dimensions (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12479">#12479</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/12454">#12454</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦Â Bug fix: Images respect center alignment in containers (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12495">#12495</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/12435">#12435</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸŒÂ Bug fix: If you use an empty string as a section label in top navigation, those pages will display individually before the collapsible sections (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12247">#12247</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/12243">#12243</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ•¸ï¸Â Bug fix: To fix a performance regression, dataframes use <code>.iat[]</code> instead of <code>.iloc[]</code> internally (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12422">#12422</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/10952">#10952</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦—Â Bug fix: <code>st.data_editor</code> accepts Shift+Enter for multiline entry in a cell (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12401">#12401</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/12386">#12386</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦‚Â Bug fix: To make <code>st.pdf</code> more compatible on Windows, MIME types were updated (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12399">#12399</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/12387">#12387</a>). Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/geoextra">geoextra</a>!</li>
<li>ğŸ¦ŸÂ Bug fix: To prevent long-word overflow, words are forced to break if they exceed their container&#x27;s width (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12370">#12370</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/12366">#12366</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦ Â Bug fix: Hiding all dataframe columns won&#x27;t raise a TypeError (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12361">#12361</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/12227">#12227</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸª°Â Bug fix: <code>st.logo</code> doesn&#x27;t dislocate the sidebar collapse button (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12329">#12329</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/12326">#12326</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸª³Â Bug fix: When usingÂ <code>accept_new_options=True</code>Â withÂ <code>st.multiselect</code>, mobile users can access their keyboards (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12330">#12330</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ•·ï¸Â Bug fix: <code>st.components.v1.html</code> ignores fractional pixels in <code>width</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12354">#12354</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/12340">#12340</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸÂ Bug fix: <code>st.number_input</code> correctly accepts keyed entries (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12351">#12351</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/12349">#12349</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸÂ Bug fix: Markdown images maintain their aspect ratio when constrained (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12343">#12343</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸœÂ Bug fix: <code>st.date_input</code> is inclusive of min and max values (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12295">#12295</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/12293">#12293</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸª²Â Bug fix: Maintain image proportions in fullscreen mode for all width settings (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12235">#12235</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ›Â Bug fix: Markdown code blocks don&#x27;t overflow when used in labels (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12175">#12175</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/12149">#12149</a>).</li>

<p><em>Release date: August 26, 2025</em></p>
<p><strong>Highlights</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ“„Â Introducing <a href="/develop/api-reference/media/st.pdf"><code>st.pdf</code></a> to beautifully render PDF documents in your app!</li>
<li>â›ï¸Â Dataframes support <a href="/develop/api-reference/data/st.dataframe#dataframeselectionstate">cell selections</a>!</li>
<li>âœ¨Â You can add sparklines to <a href="/develop/api-reference/data/st.metric"><code>st.metric</code></a>!</li>
<li>âœï¸Â <a href="/develop/api-reference/data/st.column_config/st.column_config.listcolumn"><code>ListColumn</code></a> is now editable!</li>
<li>ğŸ“‚Â Users can upload a directory of files with <a href="/develop/api-reference/widgets/st.file_uploader"><code>st.file_uploader</code></a> or <a href="/develop/api-reference/chat/st.chat_input"><code>st.chat_input</code></a>.</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Notable Changes</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ·ï¸Â You can configure the labels of options in <a href="/develop/api-reference/data/st.column_config/st.column_config.selectboxcolumn"><code>SelectboxColumn</code></a> with a new <code>format_func</code> parameter (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12232">#12232</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/6795">#6795</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸÂ You can configure the duration of <a href="/develop/api-reference/status/st.toast"><code>st.toast</code></a> messages (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11872">#11872</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/7047">#7047</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ”‘Â <a href="/develop/api-reference/execution-flow/st.form_submit_button"><code>st.form_submit_button</code></a> has a <code>key</code> parameter (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12190">#12190</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/12121">#12121</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸŒ»Â <a href="/develop/api-reference/text/st.markdown">Markdown</a> and heading dividers can be yellow (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12201">#12201</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ’¬Â <a href="/develop/api-reference/execution-flow/st.dialog"><code>st.dialog</code></a> widths have a larger option (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12040">#12040</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8904">#8904</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ’»Â <code>st.dataframe</code> and <code>st.data_editor</code> have <code>width</code> and <code>height</code> to use with flex layouts (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11930">#11930</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ–¼ï¸Â <code>st.image</code>, <code>st.pyplot</code>, and <code>st.graphviz_chart</code> have a <code>width</code> parameter to use them with flex layouts (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11952">#11952</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12212">#12212</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ“ˆÂ Users can access the underlying data of a Vega chart through the toolbar. This includes all data passed to the chart, even if it&#x27;s not displayed (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10311">#10311</a>).</li>
<li>â˜ ï¸Â <code>st.bokeh_chart</code> is deprecated. Use the <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit-bokeh"><code>streamlit-bokeh</code></a> custom component instead.</li>
<li>ğŸ§¹Â We removed deprecated commands and parameters: <code>st.experimental_dialog</code>, <code>st.experimental_fragment</code>, and caching&#x27;s <code>experimental_allow_widgets</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12167">#12167</a>).</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Other Changes</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸƒâ€â™‚ï¸Â For better performance, <code>st.slider</code> will not rerun the app until the user releases the slider thumb (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11879">#11879</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/4541">#4541</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ’…Â For improved custom theming, single mark charts use the first categorical chart color (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12162">#12162</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸŒÂ ForÂ <code>st.logo</code>, theÂ <code>crossorigin</code>Â property can be configured by hosts (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12226">#12226</a>).</li>

<li>ğŸ‘»Â The copy-to-clipboard function of multiple elements gives a checkmark feedback to users when they copy something (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12141">#12141</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12172">#12172</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ«¥Â Users can quickly hide or unhide all columns in a dataframe (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12164">#12164</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/12082">#12082</a>). Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/plumol">plumol</a>!</li>
<li>â„¹ï¸ Material icons were updated (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12264">#12264</a>).</li>

<p><em>Release date: August 5, 2025</em></p>
<p><strong>Highlights</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ’ªÂ Announcing horizontal flex <a href="/develop/api-reference/layout/st.container">containers</a>! Configure the alignment, direction, and gap of containers to create dynamic layouts.</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Notable Changes</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸªµÂ <a href="/develop/api-reference/user/st.logout"><code>st.logout</code></a> will log the user out of their identity provider if the server metadata includes <code>end_session_endpoint</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11901">#11901</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/11900">#11900</a>). Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/velochy">velochy</a>!</li>
<li>ğŸ’¬Â You can configure the dismissibility of <a href="/develop/api-reference/execution-flow/st.dialog"><code>st.dialog</code></a> and set callback functions (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9504">#9504</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12034">#12034</a>). Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/souvikmaji">souvikmaji</a>!</li>
<li>â†”ï¸Â You can set a <code>width</code> parameter for <a href="/develop/api-reference/widgets/st.button">buttons</a> and <a href="/develop/api-reference/layout/st.popover">popovers</a>.</li>
<li>ğŸ§‘â€ğŸ’»Â <a href="/develop/api-reference/configuration/config.toml#sidebar-theme"><code>codeFontWeight</code></a> can be configured separately in the sidebar.</li>
<li>ğŸ“¶Â You can configure the WebSocket ping interval with the <a href="/develop/api-reference/configuration/config.toml#server"><code>server.websocketPingInterval</code></a> configuration option (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12117">#12117</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/12108">#12108</a>).</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Other Changes</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸŒ€Â The spinner design was unified across Streamlit commands (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12031">#12031</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ’…Â Design and style tweaks (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12032">#12032</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11989">#11989</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11986">#11986</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11999">#11999</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12015">#12015</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11995">#11995</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11981">#11981</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11964">#11964</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ”„Â Error logic and logging was improved to reduce confusion from <code>asyncio</code> runtime errors when unrelated errors are raised (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12008">#12008</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸª§Â Dataframe column menus include an icon to show the column type and a button to copy the column name (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11303">#11303</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ’½Â For convenience, there are additional &quot;extras&quot; installation options (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11760">#11760</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8233">#8233</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ“Â Additional checks are performed to validate the extension of uploaded files, but app developers are still responsible for checking and handling the security of uploaded files (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11884">#11884</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/11883">#11883</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ”˜Â Button group widgets are identified by their command name in error messages (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11769">#11769</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/11753">#11753</a>). Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/bajajku">bajajku</a>!</li>
<li>âš”ï¸Â For <code>st.snow</code>, <code>st.balloons</code>, chat avatars, and media elements, the <code>crossorigin</code> property can be configured by hosts (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12087">#12087</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11948">#11948</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦—Â Bug fix: Ctrl+C will stop a Streamlit server in Windows, even if there is no active session (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12049">#12049</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/6855">#6855</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦‚Â Bug fix: <code>st.line_chart</code> uses the column order in the chart data instead of reordering them alphabetically (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12092">#12092</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/12071">#12071</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦ŸÂ Bug fix: Menu items set in <code>st.set_page_config</code> are not hidden when <code>client.toolbarMode</code> is set to <code>&quot;minimal&quot;</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12091">#12091</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/12083">#12083</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦ Â Bug fix: <code>theme.codeFontWeight</code> does not interfere with bold inline code (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12074">#12074</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/11976">#11976</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸª°Â Bug fix: To allow fractional pixel values, heading font sizes in theming configuration aren&#x27;t rounded (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12077">#12077</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/11963">#11963</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸª³Â Bug fix: Altair 5.4.0 and 5.4.1 have been excluded to prevent an upstream bug with reading dataframes (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12066">#12066</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/12064">#12064</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ•·ï¸Â Bug fix: Dataframe scrollbars have been tweaked to avoid sizing problems (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11936">#11936</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/11921">#11921</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/12053">#12053</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/11985">#11985</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸÂ Bug fix: Linting accepts lists in addition to tuples for callback arguments in widgets (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12039">#12039</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸÂ Bug fix: To fix a deprecation warning, Altair theme syntax was updated (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12050">#12050</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸœÂ Bug fix: <code>st.navigation</code> does not hide the menu when a single section is used with <code>position=&quot;top&quot;</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12025">#12025</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/12029">#12029</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸª²Â Bug fix: The sidebar state does not reset when the window is resized (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/12024">#12024</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/12016">#12016</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ›Â Bug fix: <code>st.pills</code> and <code>st.segmented_control</code> don&#x27;t raise unintended <code>StreamlitDuplicateElementId</code> errors (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11982">#11982</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/11975">#11975</a>).</li>

<p><em>Release date: July 16, 2025</em></p>
<p><strong>Highlights</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ¨Â Streamlit has additional <a href="/develop/api-reference/configuration/config.toml#theme">theming configuration</a> options!<!-- -->
<ul>
<li><code>theme.baseFontWeight</code>: Set the root font weight of text in the app.</li>
<li><code>theme.chartCategoricalColors</code>: Configure default categorical colors for Plotly, Altair, and Vega-Lite charts.</li>
<li><code>theme.chartSequentialColors</code>: Configure default sequential colors for Plotly, Altair, and Vega-Lite charts.</li>
<li><code>theme.codeFontWeight</code>: Set the font weight of code text.</li>
<li><code>theme.dataframeHeaderBackgroundColor</code>: Set the background color of dataframe headers.</li>
<li><code>theme.headingFontSizes</code>: Set the font sizes of headings.</li>
<li><code>theme.headingFontWeights</code>: Set the font weights of headings.</li>
<li><code>theme.linkUnderline</code>: Configure whether to underline links.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Notable Changes</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ’¬Â You can set the unsubmitted value of <a href="/develop/api-reference/chat/st.chat_input"><code>st.chat_input</code></a> through Session State (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10175">#10175</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/7166">#7166</a>).</li>
<li>â†”ï¸Â You can set a <code>width</code> parameter for <a href='/develop/api-reference/text/st.html'><code>st.html</code></a>, <a href="/develop/api-reference/widgets/st.feedback"><code>st.feedback</code></a>, <a href="/develop/api-reference/widgets/st.pills"><code>st.pills</code></a>, <a href="/develop/api-reference/widgets/st.segmented_control"><code>st.segmented_control</code></a>, and <a href="/develop/api-reference/widgets/st.multiselect"><code>st.multiselect</code></a>.</li>
<li>â†•ï¸Â You can set a <code>height</code> parameter for <a href="/develop/api-reference/data/st.metric"><code>st.metric</code></a> and <a href="/develop/api-reference/widgets/st.text_area"><code>st.text_area</code></a>.</li>
<li>ğŸ‘©â€ğŸ’»Â <a href="/develop/api-reference/text/st.code"><code>st.code</code></a> and <a href="/develop/api-reference/execution-flow/st.form"><code>st.form</code></a> can have <code>height=&quot;stretch&quot;</code>.</li>
<li>ğŸ§‘â€ğŸ’»Â <a href="/develop/api-reference/text/st.code"><code>st.code</code></a> can have <code>width=&quot;content&quot;</code>.</li>
<li>â±ï¸Â You can show the elapsed time with the spinner for cached functions using the <code>show_time</code> parameter (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11469">#11469</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/10647">#10647</a>). Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/Darkace01">Darkace01</a>!</li>
<li><code>server.showEmailPrompt</code> lets you configure whether to show the email prompt (for locally running apps).</li>
<li>ğŸ’¾Â <a href="/develop/api-reference/data/st.column_config/st.column_config.numbercolumn"><code>NumberColumn</code></a> and <a href="/develop/api-reference/data/st.column_config/st.column_config.progresscolumn"><code>ProgressColumn</code></a> support <code>&quot;bytes&quot;</code> as a predefined format (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11288">#11288</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/11287">#11287</a>). Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/cgivre">cgivre</a>!</li>
<li>âš™ï¸Â Column configuration accepts pixel widths for columns (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11838">#11838</a>).</li>
<li>â„¹ï¸Â The <code>display_text</code> parameter of <a href="/develop/api-reference/data/st.column_config/st.column_config.linkcolumn"><code>LinkColumn</code></a> accepts a Material icon (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11690">#11690</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/7004">#7004</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ–Šï¸Â The <code>title</code> parameter of <a href="/develop/api-reference/execution-flow/st.dialog"><code>st.dialog</code></a> accepts Markdown (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11763">#11763</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/11755">#11755</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ§©Â To support proxying requests for custom components, in <a href="/develop/api-reference/custom-components/st.components.v1.declare_component"><code>declare_component</code></a>, you can set both <code>url</code> and <code>path</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11698">#11698</a>).</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Other Changes</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ§­Â Section labels in the sidebar navigation widget are collapsible (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11863">#11863</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ“‚Â The &quot;Deploy&quot; button is hidden when the &quot;File change&quot; notification is visible in the app chrome (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11834">#11834</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ”Â When using top navigation in an app, the header has more padding (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11836">#11836</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸªœÂ In <code>NumberColumn</code>, the precision from <code>step</code> will override the display precision from <code>format</code>, unless <code>format</code> is a printf string (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11835">#11835</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ“…Â When <code>st.date_input</code> accepts a date range, the widget displays a quick-select option below the calendar for common date ranges (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10166">#10166</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/11108">#11108</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ‹ï¸Â Dataframes support font weight defined in <code>pandas</code> <code>Styler</code> objects (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11705">#11705</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/6461">#6461</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ«¥Â The about dialog does not show by default in the app menu. The current Streamlit version is displayed in the settings dialog (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10091">#10091</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ’…Â <code>st.metric</code> uses a background color for the delta value, like <code>st.badge</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11678">#11678</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ’»Â IDEs can give type hints for <code>.clear()</code> on cached functions (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11793">#11793</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11821">#11821</a>). Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/whitphx">whitphx</a>!</li>
<li>ğŸ”„Â Bug swap: To prevent a multipage app regression, <code>st.context.theme</code> does not automatically rerun the app on first load. In some cases, <code>st.context.theme</code> may not be correct until the first rerun (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11870">#11870</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/11797">#11797</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ§¹Â Bug fix: <code>st.chat_input</code> displays correctly at the bottom of the screen in mobile view (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11896">#11896</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/11722">#11722</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/11891">#11891</a>).</li>
<li>â³Â Bug fix: When a WebSocket reconnects, the app will fully rerun to prevent missing fragments (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11890">#11890</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/11660">#11660</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸª±Â Bug fix: To reduce <code>No such file or directory</code> errors, the file watcher has more robust exception handling and clearer logging (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11871">#11871</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11841">#11841</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/11809">#11809</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/11728">#11728</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ’©Â Bug fix: Vega-Lite facet charts do not flicker (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11833">#11833</a>).</li>
<li>â˜ ï¸Â Bug fix: When the initial sidebar state is set to <code>&quot;collapsed&quot;</code>, the sidebar correctly loads in a collapsed state without flickering open (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11861">#11861</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/11848">#11848</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ‘½Â Bug fix: To prevent apps from being out of sync with their current code at a later time, Streamlit clears the script cache when all file watchers disconnect (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11876">#11876</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11739">#11739</a>). Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/diwu-sf">diwu-sf</a>!</li>
<li>ğŸ‘»Â Bug fix: Inline code in tooltips has the same relative size as inline code in other Markdown text (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11877">#11877</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦€Â Bug fix: <code>st.multiselect</code> and <code>st.selectbox</code> display the correct placeholder text when <code>accept_new_options=True</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11623">#11623</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/11609">#11609</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦‹Â Bug fix: The column visibility menu can be closed by toggling the toolbar icon (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11857">#11857</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/11801">#11801</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦Â Bug fix: Progress bar columns in dataframes have the correct padding between the bar and its label (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11685">#11685</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸŒÂ Bug fix: The warning indicator in a dataframe cell adapts to theme configuration (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11682">#11682</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ•¸ï¸Â Bug fix: To fix multiple visual and UX bugs in dataframe, <code>glide-data-grid</code> was updated (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11677">#11677</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8310">#8310</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/9498">#9498</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/9471">#9471</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦—Â Bug fix: In the sidebar navigation widget, font spacing and weight were adjust for visual clarity (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11814">#11814</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦‚Â Bug fix: Altair charts correctly resize in width to match their container (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11807">#11807</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/11802">#11802</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦ŸÂ Bug fix: The running-man icon matches the theme configuration (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11461">#11461</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/11371">#11371</a>). Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/TreavVasu">TreavVasu</a>!</li>
<li>ğŸ¦ Â Bug fix: The top header background is correctly opaque when it contains elements (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11787">#11787</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/11785">#11785</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸª°Â Bug fix: Extra top padding is removed when printing (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11798">#11798</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸª³Â Bug fix: Markdown inline code displays correctly when <code>unsafe_allow_html=True</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11817">#11817</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/11800">#11800</a>). Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/bajajku">bajajku</a>!</li>
<li>ğŸ•·ï¸Â Bug fix: The WebSocket ping interval does not exceed the timeout interval (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11693">#11693</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/11670">#11670</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸÂ Bug fix: The sidebar state initialized correctly on Community Cloud and page content slides and resizes correctly in response to the sidebar (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11732">#11732</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/11702">#11702</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/11710">#11710</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸÂ Bug fix: The timer in <code>st.spinner</code> uses system time to prevent pausing when the user focuses on another browser tab (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11756">#11756</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/11720">#11720</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸœÂ Bug fix: Empty containers with borders and empty expanders are visible before elements are added to them (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11669">#11669</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸª²Â Bug fix: <code>st.audio_input</code> and <code>st.camera_input</code> have consistent appearances (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11699">#11699</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/11700">#11700</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ›Â Bug fix: To prevent a race condition, the file watcher correctly applies a lock to watched paths (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11692">#11692</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/11691">#11691</a>).</li>
</ul>

<p><em>Release date: June 18, 2025</em></p>
<p><strong>Highlights</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ§­Â Introducing top navigation! Use <a href="https://docs.streamlit.io/develop/api-reference/navigation/st.navigation"><code>st.navigation</code></a> with <code>position=&quot;top&quot;</code> to create a navigation menu across the top of your app.</li>
<li>ğŸ”†Â You can detect if the viewer is in light mode or dark mode at runtime with <a href="https://docs.streamlit.io/develop/api-reference/caching-and-state/st.context#contexttheme"><code>st.context.theme</code></a>.</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Notable Changes</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸªºÂ Streamlit no longer restricts the nesting of columns, expanders, popovers, and chat message containers, but beware of bad design! Always be mindful of different screen sizes and orientations, and don&#x27;t overuse nested layouts.</li>
<li>â†”ï¸Â You can set the width of most Streamlit elements.</li>
<li>â¬†ï¸Â <a href="https://docs.streamlit.io/develop/api-reference/execution-flow/st.form"><code>st.form</code></a> has a new parameter to configure its <code>height</code>.</li>
<li>ğŸ› ï¸Â <a href="https://docs.streamlit.io/develop/api-reference/layout/st.columns"><code>st.columns</code></a> supports <code>gap=None</code> for no gap between columns.</li>
<li>ğŸ‹ï¸Â Font face declarations in <a href="https://docs.streamlit.io/develop/api-reference/configuration/config.toml#theme"><code>config.toml</code></a> support weight and unicode ranges (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11248">#11248</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/11163">#11163</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/11247">#11247</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ˜ƒÂ Font face declarations are supported in the window variable (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11628">#11628</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/11568">#11568</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ”Â Streamlit searches for secrets and configuration options relative to the entrypoint file in addition to the working directory and user root (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10173">#10173</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8195">#8195</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¨Â A new configuration option, <code>theme.dataframeBorderColor</code>, lets you set the border color for dataframes and tables separately from other border colors (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11475">#11475</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸŒ¯Â A new configuration option, <code>theme.buttonRadius</code>, lets you set the radius of buttons separately from other elements (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11464">#11464</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ–¥ï¸ A new configuration option, <code>theme.codeFontSize</code>, lets you set the size of code in <code>st.code</code>, <code>st.json</code>, and <code>st.help</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11508">#11508</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ”’Â You can configure a list of allowed origins when CORS protection is enabled (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11377">#11377</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ“„Â <code>st.set_page_config</code> can be called multiple times in a single script run (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11286">#11286</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/4483">#4483</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/2216">#2216</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/9797">#9797</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/9038">#9038</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ—ºï¸Â <code>st.pydeck_chart</code> and <a href="http://st.map"><code>st.map</code></a> now use Carto by default to provide map tiles (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11231">#11231</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ‘€Â You can configure Streamlit to watch additional directories for changes with the new configuration option, <code>server.folderWatchList</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9656">#9656</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/9655">#9655</a>). Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/akramsystems">akramsystems</a>!</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Other Changes</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ”˜Â Exception messages include a copy button to conveniently copy the message to your clipboard (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11250">#11250</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/11083">#11083</a>). Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/snakeM">snakeM</a>!</li>
<li>âš“Â Streamlit apps can be served from port 3000 (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11525">#11525</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8149">#8149</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ‘ŸÂ Markdown dependencies were upgraded for improved performance (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11553">#11553</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/11550">#11550</a>).</li>
<li>â†”ï¸Â The sidebar is narrower by default and consistently handles the scrollbar spacing (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11412">#11412</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ‘‹Â We gave Streamlit hello a couple small tweaks (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11442">#11442</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ§‘â€ğŸ’»Â Base URL window variables are consistently namespaced in <code>__streamlit</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11481">#11481</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸŒÂ Streamlit apps now serve a <code>manifest.json</code> file (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11462">#11462</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ–Œï¸Â <code>st.dataframe</code> shows row selection boxes always instead of just on hover (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11411">#11411</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/11410">#11410</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦‹Â <code>ListColumn</code> and <code>LinkColumn</code> can inherit coloring from <code>pandas</code> <code>Styler</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11612">#11612</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8254">#8254</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ’¹Â <code>NumberColumn</code> and <code>ProgressColumn</code> support a Japanese yen number format (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11588">#11588</a>). Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/alexmalins">alexmalins</a>!</li>
<li>ğŸ”—Â <code>st.page_link</code> can inherit an icon when passed a <code>StreamlitPage</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10694">#10694</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/9743">#9743</a>). Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/abokey1">abokey1</a>!</li>
<li>ğŸ«Â A button&#x27;s placement in the sidebar or main body of an app is included in its widget identity (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10881">#10881</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/10598">#10598</a>). Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/joaooliveira-11">joaooliveira-11</a>!</li>
<li>ğŸ•·ï¸Â Built-in Streamlit fonts now use variable font files (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11646">#11646</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11600">#11600</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11534">#11534</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¤¹Â Bug fix: Streamlit Markdown correctly formats task lists and block quotes (#11237).</li>
<li>ğŸÂ Bug fix: Horizontal scroll bars are sized correctly in Safari (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11625">#11625</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸÂ Bug fix: Unnecessary media caching was reduced to improve efficiency and avoid video player crashes (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11635">#11635</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/9688">#9688</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸœÂ Bug fix: <code>st.text</code> uses the <code>break-word</code> CSS property to wrap long lines without whitespace (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10969">#10969</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/10824">#10824</a>). Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/matilde2004">matilde2004</a>!</li>
<li>ğŸª²Â Bug fix: Material icons display correctly in <code>st.markdown</code> when <code>unsafe_allow_html=True</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11633">#11633</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/9945">#9945</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ›Â Bug fix: Multi-index column names preserve brackets (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11617">#11617</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/10415">#10415</a>).</li>

<p><em>Release date: April 29, 2025</em></p>
<p><strong>Highlights</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ§‘ Announcing the general availability of <a href="https://docs.streamlit.io/develop/api-reference/user/st.user"><code>st.user</code></a>, a dict-like object to access information about the current user.</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Notable Changes</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>â• <a href="https://docs.streamlit.io/develop/api-reference/widgets/st.multiselect"><code>st.multiselect</code></a> and <a href="https://docs.streamlit.io/develop/api-reference/widgets/st.selectbox"><code>st.selectbox</code></a> have a new parameter to let users add new options.</li>
<li>ğŸ¥¸ <a href="https://docs.streamlit.io/develop/api-reference/caching-and-state/st.context"><code>st.context</code></a> has new attributes: <code>url</code>, <code>ip_address</code>, and <code>is_embedded</code>.</li>
<li>âš ï¸ Text <a href="https://docs.streamlit.io/develop/api-reference/status/st.success">alerts</a> and <a href="https://docs.streamlit.io/develop/api-reference/status/st.exception">exceptions</a> have a new <code>width</code> parameter (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11142">#11142</a>).</li>
<li>âŒ¨ï¸ You can set the tab index for <a href='https://docs.streamlit.io/develop/api-reference/custom-components/st.components.v1.html'><code>st.components.v1.html</code></a> and <a href="https://docs.streamlit.io/develop/api-reference/custom-components/st.components.v1.iframe"><code>st.components.v1.iframe</code></a> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11065">#11065</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/7969">#7969</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸŒ When you pass a CSS file&#x27;s path to <a href='https://docs.streamlit.io/develop/api-reference/text/st.html'><code>st.html</code></a>, Streamlit will automatically insert <code>&lt;style&gt;</code> tags and avoid creating extra space in the app (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10979">#10979</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/9388">#9388</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/10027">#10027</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ˜ƒ You can add an icon to the left of the value in <a href="https://docs.streamlit.io/develop/api-reference/widgets/st.text_input"><code>st.text_input</code></a> and <a href="https://docs.streamlit.io/develop/api-reference/widgets/st.number_input"><code>st.number_input</code></a>.</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Other Changes</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ—‘ï¸ Per the scheduled deprecation, <code>st.experimental_audio_input</code> has been removed. Use <code>st.audio_input</code> instead.</li>
<li>ğŸ’… Various elements received styling tweaks for consistency and compatibility with advanced theming (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10916">#10916</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10930">#10930</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10915">#10915</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10944">#10944</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10990">#10990</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11033">#11033</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11034">#11034</a>).</li>
<li>âš’ï¸ The element toolbar sizing and spacing was adjusted for improved UX (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11135">#11135</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11155">#11155</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ«¥ Bug fix: Streamlit does not display a frontend error when displaying an empty dataframe (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11100">#11100</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/11064">#11064</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ” Bug fix: <code>st.context</code> retains its information when calling <code>st.rerun</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11113">#11113</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/11111">#11111</a>).</li>

<li>ğŸ‘» Bug fix: When updating <code>config.toml</code>during development, Streamlit will elegantly handle invalid TOML formatting and reload the configuration file on the next save (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10857">#10857</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/1256">#1256</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8320">#8320</a>).</li>

<li>ğŸ¦€ Bug fix: Streamlit ignores <code>__init__.py</code> and dotfiles in the <code>/pages</code> directory when automatically declaring pages in a multipage app (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11009">#11009</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/11006">#11006</a>).</li>
<li>â© <code>st.write</code> received an optimization tweak for rendering strings (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10985">#10985</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦ Bug fix: <code>st.html</code> renders at 100% width for correct sizing (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10976">#10976</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/10964">#10964</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸŒ Bug fix: Page links become disabled if a client disconnects from the Streamlit server (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10946">#10946</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/9198">#9198</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ•¸ï¸ Bug fix: Streamlit supports newer emojis in page icons (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10912">#10912</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/11154">#11154</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦— Bug fix: <code>st.exception</code> only shows links to Google and ChatGPT when the app is being accessed through <a href="http://localhost"><code>localhost</code></a> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10971">#10971</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/10924">#10924</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦‚ Bug fix: <code>st.chat_input</code> will expand to show multi-line placeholder text in most browsers. Firefox does not support this fix (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10931">#10931</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/10611">#10611</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦Ÿ Bug fix: Streamlit elegantly catches a <code>TypeError</code> when concurrent changes to rows and columns cause a failure in serialization (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10954">#10954</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/10937">#10937</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦  Bug fix: Streamlit cleanly handles non-ASCII characters in anchor links, which may change some anchors in existing apps (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10925">#10929</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8114">#8114</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸª° Bug fix: To prevent a race condition, session information is not immediately cleared unless a new session message is received (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9886">#9886</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/9767">#9767</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸª³ Bug fix: <code>streamlit config show</code> correctly displays <code>client.showErrorDetails</code> as a string instead of a list (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10921">#10921</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/10913">#10913</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ•·ï¸ Bug fix: <code>st.selectbox</code> does not lose its value if a partial edit is abandoned (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10891">#10891</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ Bug fix: <code>st.badge</code> doesn&#x27;t falsely show <code>rainbow</code> as a color option (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10896">#10896</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ Bug fix: To avoid a file lock conflict the occurs with some IDEs, Streamlit&#x27;s file watcher utilities retries reading files when blocked (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10868">#10868</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/4486">#4486</a>). Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/Morridin">Morridin</a>!</li>
<li>ğŸœ Bug fix: <code>st.selectbox</code> and <code>st.multiselect</code> have consistent color and spacing for placeholder text (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10865">#10865</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸª² Bug fix: Context managers correctly handle form elements (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10752">#10752</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8761">#8761</a>). Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/SrGesus">SrGesus</a>!</li>
<li>ğŸ› Bug fix: <code>st.link_button</code> and <code>st.tabs</code> remain active when a client disconnects from a Streamlit server (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10861">#10861</a>).</li>
</ul>

<p><em>Release date: March 25, 2025</em></p>
<p><strong>Highlights</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ’ˆÂ Introducing <a href="/develop/api-reference/configuration/config.toml#theme">advanced theming options</a>! Use an assortment of configuration options to customize the appearance of your app. Change the fonts, colors, and roundness of your app without CSS.</li>
<li>ğŸ‘®Â Introducing <a href="/develop/api-reference/text/st.badge"><code>st.badge</code></a> to insert a colored badge element. You can also include badges in Markdown using a new directive.</li>
<li>ğŸ—ï¸Â Use <a href="/develop/api-reference/cli/init"><code>streamlit init</code></a> in your terminal to create all the local files you need for a new Streamlit app.</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Notable Changes</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ¤–Â <a href="/develop/api-reference/status/st.exception"><code>st.exception</code></a> includes links to open Google or ChatGPT with the contents of the exception. This includes uncaught exceptions displayed in the app.</li>
<li>ğŸ—ºï¸Â You can access the user&#x27;s locale through <a href="/develop/api-reference/caching-and-state/st.context#contextlocale"><code>st.context</code></a> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10563">#10563</a>).</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Other Changes</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ“„Â When using a <code>pages/</code> directory to automatically generate a multipage app, no pages (including the entrypoint file) can have the same inferred URL pathname (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10276">#10276</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸï¸Â To improve performance, Streamlit uses the React 18 <code>createRoot</code> API for its frontend (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10453">#10453</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ“Â To improve compatibility with AI tools, script compilation errors are logged when <code>logger.level=&quot;error&quot;</code> and not just when <code>logger.level=&quot;debug&quot;</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10826">#10826</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸªµÂ Streamlit automatically enables more detailed logging if <code>rich</code> is installed (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10650">#10650</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ”¢Â <code>st.slider</code> and <code>st.number_input</code> raise an error when assigned a value in excess of a declared minimum or maximum (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9964">#9964</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/9342">#9342</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ› ï¸Â <code>st.table</code> support pandas <code>Styler.set_tooltips()</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10561">#10561</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/10553">#10553</a>).</li>
<li>â„¹ï¸Â Material symbols have been updated to the latest icon set (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10813">#10813</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10717">#10717</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦‹Â Visual tweaks to headers (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10599">#10599</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦€Â Bug fix: <code>st.html</code> displays correctly when used inside <code>st.tabs</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10825">#10825</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/10815">#10815</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦Â Bug fix: For backwards compatibility, <code>theme.font=&quot;sans serfi&quot;</code> is internally converted to the new <code>theme.font=&quot;sans-serif&quot;</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10789">#10789</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/10786">#10786</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸŒÂ Bug fix: When using <code>st.secrets</code>, if Streamlit can&#x27;t find the <code>secrets.toml</code> file, it will raise a <code>FileNotFoundError</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10508">#10508</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8559">#8559</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ•¸ï¸Â Bug fix: <code>st.secrets</code> raises a clear <code>TypeError</code> if you try to assign a value to an attribute (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10698">#10698</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/10107">#10107</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦—Â Bug fix: In single-page apps, <code>st.page_link</code> does not highlight external links as if they are the current page (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10690">#10690</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/10689">#10689</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦‚Â Bug fix: <code>st.poppover</code> displays at the correct width when using the <code>help</code> parameter (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10709">#10709</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/10693">#10693</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦ŸÂ Bug fix: All components (and custom components) that read their width from the DOM initially load with a width of -1 px to prevent flickering (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10712">#10712</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10672">#10672</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10663">#10663</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/10644">#10644</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦ Â Bug fix: When <code>st.number_input</code> is configured to use integers, the default minimum and maximum values will prevent integer overflow (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10655">#10655</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/6740">#6740</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸª°Â Bug fix: <code>st.navigation</code> uses immutable types to prevent mypy errors (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10670">#10670</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸª³Â Bug fix: Custom components correctly inherit font from theme configuration (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10661">#10661</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/10660">#10660</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ•·ï¸Â Bug fix: Dataframes correctly support Dask data objects (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10662">#10662</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸÂ Bug fix: Button widths are correct when using the <code>help</code> parameter (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10658">#10658</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/10648">#10648</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/10656">#10656</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸÂ Bug fix: Scrolling is disabled when hovering over <code>st.number_input</code> to prevent accidental value changes (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10642">#10642</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8867">#8867</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸœÂ Bug fix: <code>st.chat_input</code> gives a clear error in the UI when the file size limit is exceeded (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10530">#10530</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸª²Â Bug fix: The favicon and Markdown emojis use the same SVG emoji source for consistency (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10539">#10539</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/6822">#6822</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ›Â Bug fix: The dataframe search bar is more responsive to width (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10534">#10534</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/10532">#10532</a>).</li>
</ul>
