<p><em>Release date: March 4, 2025</em></p>
<p><strong>Highlights</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ“Â Announcing the option to accept files with <a href="/develop/api-reference/chat/st.chat_input"><code>st.chat_input</code></a>!</li>
<li>ğŸ“’ Introducing a new column type for column configuration! Use <a href="/develop/api-reference/data/st.column_config/st.column_config.jsoncolumn"><code>JsonColumn</code></a> to show JSON-compatible objects.</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Notable Changes</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸƒÂ You can prevent <a href="/develop/api-reference/widgets/st.download_button"><code>st.download_button</code></a> from triggering a rerun by setting <code>on_click=&quot;ignore&quot;</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10296">#10296</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/4382">#4382</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ•‘Â You can access a user&#x27;s timezone and timezone offset through <a href="/develop/api-reference/caching-and-state/st.context"><code>st.context</code></a> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10336">#10336</a>).</li>
<li>â†•ï¸Â You can configure the row height in <a href="/develop/api-reference/data/st.dataframe"><code>st.dataframe</code></a> and <a href="/develop/api-reference/data/st.data_editor"><code>st.data_editor</code></a> with a new parameter (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9549">#9549</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/7266">#7266</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8632">#8632</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/5386">#5386</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ’…Â <code>st.dataframe</code> and <code>st.data_editor</code> use <code>use_container_width=True</code> by default (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10434">#10434</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¤Â <a href="/develop/api-reference/text/st.markdown">Markdown</a> has a small text directive (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10487">#10487</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/10486">#10486</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ§µÂ You can pass strings, paths, and callables to <a href="/develop/api-reference/navigation/st.navigation"><code>st.navigation</code></a> in place of <code>StreamlitPage</code> objects for convenience (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10358">#10358</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/10069">#10069</a>). Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/ashm-dev">ashm-dev</a>!</li>
<li>ğŸ“ˆÂ Streamlit has a new custom component, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit-bokeh"><code>streamlit-bokeh</code></a>, to support the latest version of Bokeh (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10374">#10374</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/5858">#5858</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ”£Â <a href="/develop/api-reference/data/st.column_config/st.column_config.numbercolumn"><code>NumberColumn</code></a>, <a href="/develop/api-reference/data/st.column_config/st.column_config.progresscolumn"><code>ProgressColumn</code></a>, <a href="/develop/api-reference/data/st.column_config/st.column_config.datetimecolumn"><code>DatetimeColumn</code></a>, <a href="/develop/api-reference/data/st.column_config/st.column_config.datecolumn"><code>DateColumn</code></a>, and <a href="/develop/api-reference/data/st.column_config/st.column_config.timecolumn"><code>TimeColumn</code></a> have preconfigured format options for ease of use (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10179">#10179</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8788">#8788</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/7702">#7702</a>).</li>

</ul>
<p><strong>Other Changes</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ¥·Â Users can hide dataframe columns (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10264">#10264</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/6870">#6870</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ“…Â Users can change the format of numbers, dates, and times in dataframes (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10420">#10420</a>).</li>
<li>â†”ï¸Â Users can auto-size column widths (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10476">#10476</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ»â€â„ï¸Â Streamlit supports Polars dataframe and series hashing (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10408">#10408</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/10347">#10347</a>).</li>
<li>â˜ ï¸Â <code>rich</code> is no longer a required dependency for Streamlit (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10320">#10320</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦‹Â <code>st.file_uploader</code> has a better display format in narrow containers (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10272">#10272</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦Â Bug fix: Tabs are prevented from having a width of zero to prevent flickering (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10533">#10533</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸŒÂ Bug fix: Column order is correctly displayed when set in column configuration (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10445">#10445</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/10442">#10442</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ•¸ï¸Â Bug fix: We updated dataframe null handling to prevent deprecation warnings (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10484">#10484</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦—Â Bug fix: Elapsed time doesn&#x27;t overflow for <code>st.audio_input</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10410">#10410</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/10373">#10373</a>). Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/ashm-dev">ashm-dev</a>!</li>
<li>ğŸ¦‚Â Bug fix: <code>st.altair_chart</code> does not show an incorrect &quot;true&quot; tooltip when the user makes a selection (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10456">#10456</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/10448">#10448</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦ŸÂ Bug fix: Streamlit does not raise a RuntimeError when an <code>asyncio</code> event loop is not already running (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10455">#10455</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/10452">#10452</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦ Â Bug fix: The key for an internal MIME type is set correctly to avoid a browser warning (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10404">#10404</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸª°Â Bug fix: <code>st.data_editor</code> automatically scrolls to the bottom when a user adds a row (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10405">#10405</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/10351">#10351</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸª³Â Bug fix: Tooltips are suppressed on user-added rows in <code>st.data_editor</code> to prevent erroneous warnings (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10398">#10398</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ•·ï¸Â Bug fix: <code>st.logo</code> displays consistently when used with fragments and dialogs (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10377">#10377</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/10350">#10350</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/10382">#10382</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸÂ Bug fix: <code>st.graphviz_chart</code> has rounded corners for consistent style (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10224">#10224</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸÂ Bug fix: Streamlit raises a clear exception when an underscore is used in <code>provider</code> for <code>st.login</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10360">#10360</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/10356">#10356</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸœÂ Bug fix: The dataframe column menu displays correctly inside dialogs (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10359">#10359</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/10357">#10357</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸª²Â Bug fix: Exception handling was adjusted for improved compatibility with Cython (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10354">#10354</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/10353">#10353</a>). Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/tutu-sol">tutu-sol</a>!</li>
<li>ğŸ›Â Bug fix: <code>st.pills</code> and <code>st.segmented_control</code> have consistent font sizes across browsers (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10349">#10349</a>).</li>
</ul>

<p><em>Release date: February 4, 2025</em></p>
<p><strong>Highlights</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ‘©â€ğŸ’»Â Introducing <a href="/develop/api-reference/user/st.login"><code>st.login()</code></a> and <a href="/develop/api-reference/user/st.logout"><code>st.logout()</code></a> to authenticate users with any OpenID Connect provider.</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Notable Changes</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>â£ï¸Â <a href="/develop/api-reference/data/st.table"><code>st.table</code></a> supports Markdown (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8785">#8785</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10088">#10088</a>).</li>
<li>â²ï¸Â <a href="/develop/api-reference/status/st.spinner"><code>st.spinner</code></a> can show elapsed time with <code>show_time=True</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/6805">#6805</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10072">#10072</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ’ˆÂ <a href="/develop/api-reference/media/st.image"><code>st.image</code></a> supports Markdown in the <code>caption</code> parameter (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/6808">#6808</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10075">#10075</a>).</li>
<li>â†•ï¸Â <a href="/develop/api-reference/text/st.code"><code>st.code</code></a> has a <code>height</code> parameter (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/7418">#7418</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10080">#10080</a>).</li>
<li>â†”ï¸Â Most charts default to using <code>use_container_width=True</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10064">#10064</a>).</li>
<li>â„ï¸Â <a href="/develop/api-reference/connections/st.connections.snowflakeconnection"><code>SnowflakeConnection</code></a> was updated to match the current Snowflake API, which changes its handling of keyword arguments in some cases (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10122">#10122</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸÂ Users can drag and drop dataframe columns to rearrange them (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8796">#8796</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10099">#10099</a>).</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Other Changes</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ“ŒÂ Dataframes have column menus for users to sort and pin columns (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10206">#10206</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸš¦Â Dataframes support categorical indices (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/9647">#9647</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10195">#10195</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ›¸Â Dataframes show a hover highlight on rows (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8096">#8096</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10104">#10104</a>).</li>
<li>âš ï¸Â When dataframes have cell values that are inconsistent with their configured type, Streamlit shows a tooltip describing the error (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8253">#8253</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9899">#9899</a>).</li>
<li>â° If there is an existing asyncio event loop when a Streamlit app starts, the app will reuse it instead of creating a new one (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10164">#10164</a>). Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/DeltaGa">DeltaGa</a>!</li>
<li>ğŸ–¼ï¸Â Streamlit recognizes <code>pyspark.sql.connect.dataframe.DataFrame</code> objects as dataframes (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/9953">#9953</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9954">#9954</a>). Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/OSalama">OSalama</a>!</li>
<li>ğŸ˜ƒÂ We&#x27;ve updated emoji validation for new emojis (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10149">#10149</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ”£Â Material Symbols have been updated with the latest icons (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10247">#10247</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ’…Â Visual tweaks and improvements (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8705">#8705</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9823">#9823</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10047">#10047</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10048">#10048</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10083">#10083</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10087">#10087</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10225">#10225</a>).</li>
<li>â­•Â <code>st.image</code> displays rounded corners for consistent design (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9999">#9999</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ©Â Bug fix: Top margin is applied correctly in <code>st.columns</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/10265">#10265</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10268">#10268</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ’©Â Bug fix: <code>react-syntax-highlighter</code> is aliased to prevent rendering errors in <code>st.code</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/10231">#10231</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10244">#10244</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ§¹Â Bug fix: We improved error messages for <code>st.query_params</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/10111">#10111</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10237">#10237</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸª±Â Bug fix: Linting for <code>st.altair_chart</code> recognizes all Altair chart types (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10202">#10202</a>).</li>
<li>â†—ï¸Â Bug fix: <code>st.dataframe</code> supports raw Arrow data (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/5606">#5606</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10191">#10191</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸÂ Bug fix: <code>st.navigation</code> and <code>st.page_link</code> work when running in pure Python tests (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10163">#10163</a>).</li>
<li>â˜ ï¸Â Bug fix: Retries were added to prevent a possible race condition when files are removed while Streamlit is running (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10148">#10148</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ‘½Â Bug fix: When printing an app, <code>st.logo</code> will only print once (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/10165">#10165</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10171">#10171</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸŒÂ Bug fix: Material icons are marked to prevent translation (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/10168">#10168</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10174">#10174</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ‘»Â Bug fix: <code>st.vega_lite_chart</code> correctly caches and updates its data (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/6689">#6689</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10125">#10125</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦€Â Bug fix: When a fragment ID is not found, Streamlit logs a warning but doesn&#x27;t raise an error (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/9921">#9921</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10130">#10130</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦‹Â Bug fix: The label on <code>st.expander</code> correctly fades when stale (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10085">#10085</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦Â Bug fix: <code>st.date_input</code> provides better type hinting for its return value (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/9477">#9477</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9620">#9620</a>). Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/pranaybattu">pranaybattu</a>!</li>
<li>ğŸŒÂ Bug fix: In dataframes, small float values display their first significant figure instead of displaying as 0 (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10060">#10060</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ•¸ï¸Â Bug fix: When <code>rich</code> is installed, errors are only logged once. (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10097">#10097</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦—Â Bug fix: <code>st.text</code> preserves whitespace (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/10055">#10055</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10062">#10062</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦‚Â Bug fix: Dataframe <code>width</code> is not ignored when <code>height</code> is changed (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/9762">#9762</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10036">#10036</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦ŸÂ Bug fix: Multi index columns correctly handle empty labels (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/9749">#9749</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10035">#10035</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦ Â Bug fix: Pinned columns respect <code>column_order</code> in when configured in <code>st.dataframe</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/9997">#9997</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10034">#10034</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸª°Â Bug fix: Tooltips don&#x27;t overflow to the left or right (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/9288">#9288</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/9452">#9452</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9983">#9983</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸª³Â Bug fix: Disabled feedback widgets correctly show their value (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10030">#10030</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ•·ï¸Â Bug fix: Widgets correctly submit values if a user edits the value and immediately clicks a button (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/10007">#10007</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10018">#10018</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸÂ Bug fix: Some MIME types have been hardcoded to protect against browser misconfiguration (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/10004">#10004</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10010">#10010</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸÂ Bug fix: Files that unnecessarily inflated Streamlit&#x27;s installation size were removed (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/10008">#10008</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10011">#10011</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸœÂ Bug fix: <code>st.date_input</code> gives the correct type hint for the <code>value</code> parameter (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/10005">#10005</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/10006">#10006</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸª²Â Bug fix: <code>st.write</code> passes to <code>st.html</code> when <code>._repr_html()</code> is present for an object (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9910">#9910</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ›Â Bug fix: <code>st.html</code> preserves <code>target=_blank</code> if set in an HTML string (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/9972">#9972</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9994">#9994</a>).</li>
